18 package org.apache.maven.unbound
19 
20 import com.typesafe.config.{ Config, ConfigObject }
21 import net.ceedubs.ficus.Ficus._
22 import net.ceedubs.ficus.readers.ArbitraryTypeReader._
23 import net.ceedubs.ficus.readers.ValueReader
24 
25 /**
26   * This trait provides the ability to read Maven POM projects from Typesafe
27   * Config objects.  Since the Typesafe ConfigFactory provides so many ways
28   * to read Typesafe Config objects, only the Config -> Maven POM case class
29   * is provided here.  Ficus is used to automate much of the conversion.
30   */
31 trait HoconProjectReader {
32 
33   import SL._
34 
35   // code to convert some of the more complex POM case classes from Config
36   // objects
37   implicit val developerConfigReader: ValueReader[Developer] =
38     ValueReader.relative { config =>
39       Developer(
40         if (config.hasPath(Id)) config.as[String](Id) else null,
41         if (config.hasPath(Name)) config.as[String](Name) else null,
42         if (config.hasPath(Email)) config.as[String](Email) else null,
43         if (config.hasPath(UrlStr)) config.as[String](UrlStr) else null,
44         if (config.hasPath(OrganizationStr)) config.as[String](OrganizationStr)
45         else null,
46         if (config.hasPath(OrganizationUrl)) config.as[String](OrganizationUrl)
47         else null,
48         if (config.hasPath(Roles)) config.as[Seq[String]](Roles)
49         else Seq[String](),
50         if (config.hasPath(TimezoneStr)) config.as[String](TimezoneStr)
51         else null,
52         if (config.hasPath(PropertiesStr))
53           config.as[Map[String, String]](PropertiesStr)
54         else Map[String, String]()
55       )
56     }
57 
58   implicit val contributorConfigReader: ValueReader[Contributor] =
59     ValueReader.relative { config =>
60       Contributor(
61         if (config.hasPath(Name)) config.as[String](Name) else null,
62         if (config.hasPath(Email)) config.as[String](Email) else null,
63         if (config.hasPath(UrlStr)) config.as[String](UrlStr) else null,
64         if (config.hasPath(OrganizationStr)) config.as[String](OrganizationStr)
65         else null,
66         if (config.hasPath(OrganizationUrl)) config.as[String](OrganizationUrl)
67         else null,
68         if (config.hasPath(Roles)) config.as[Seq[String]](Roles)
69         else Seq[String](),
70         if (config.hasPath(TimezoneStr)) config.as[String](TimezoneStr)
71         else null,
72         if (config.hasPath(PropertiesStr))
73           config.as[Map[String, String]](PropertiesStr)
74         else Map[String, String]()
75       )
76     }
77 
78   implicit val ciManagementConfigReader: ValueReader[CIManagement] =
79     ValueReader.relative { config =>
80       CIManagement(
81         if (config.hasPath(SystemStr)) config.getString(SystemStr) else null,
82         if (config.hasPath(UrlStr)) config.getString(UrlStr) else null,
83         if (config.hasPath(Notifiers)) config.as[Seq[Notifier]](Notifiers)
84         else Seq[Notifier]()
85       )
86     }
87 
88   implicit val notifierConfigReader: ValueReader[Notifier] =
89     ValueReader.relative { config =>
90       Notifier(
91         if (config.hasPath(TypeStr)) config.getString(TypeStr) else Mail,
92         if (config.hasPath(SendOnError))
93           config.getBoolean(SendOnError)
94         else true,
95         if (config.hasPath(SendOnFailure))
96           config.getBoolean(SendOnFailure)
97         else true,
98         if (config.hasPath(SendOnSuccess))
99           config.getBoolean(SendOnSuccess)
100         else true,
101         if (config.hasPath(SendOnWarning))
102           config.getBoolean(SendOnWarning)
103         else true,
104         if (config.hasPath(Configuration))
105           config.as[Map[String, String]](Configuration)
106         else Map[String, String]()
107       )
108     }
109 
110   implicit val profileConfigReader: ValueReader[Profile] =
111     ValueReader.relative { config =>
112       Profile(
113         if (config.hasPath(Id)) config.as[String](Id) else null,
114         if (config.hasPath(ActivationStr))
115           config.as[Activation](ActivationStr)
116         else null,
117         if (config.hasPath(BuildStr)) config.as[BuildBase](BuildStr) else null,
118         if (config.hasPath(Modules)) config.as[Seq[String]](Modules)
119         else Seq[String](),
120         if (config.hasPath(DistributionManagementStr))
121           config.as[DistributionManagement](DistributionManagementStr)
122         else null,
123         if (config.hasPath(PropertiesStr))
124           config.as[Map[String, String]](PropertiesStr)
125         else null,
126         if (config.hasPath(DependencyManagementStr))
127           config.as[Seq[Dependency]](DependencyManagementStr)
128         else null,
129         if (config.hasPath(Dependencies))
130           config.as[Seq[Dependency]](Dependencies)
131         else null,
132         if (config.hasPath(Repositories))
133           config.as[Seq[Repository]](Repositories)
134         else null,
135         if (config.hasPath(PluginRepositories))
136           config.as[Seq[Repository]](PluginRepositories)
137         else null,
138         if (config.hasPath(ReportingStr)) config.as[Reporting](ReportingStr)
139         else null
140       )
141     }
142 
143   implicit val manifestSectionConfigReader: ValueReader[ManifestSection] =
144     ValueReader.relative { config =>
145       ManifestSection(
146         if (config.hasPath(Name)) config.as[String](Name) else null,
147         if (config.hasPath(ManifestEntries))
148           config.as[Map[String, String]](ManifestEntries)
149         else null
150       )
151     }
152 
153   implicit val distributionManagementConfigReader:
154       ValueReader[DistributionManagement] =
155     ValueReader.relative { config =>
156       DistributionManagement(
157         if (config.hasPath(RepositoryStr))
158           config.as[DeploymentRepository](RepositoryStr)
159         else null,
160         if (config.hasPath(SnapshotRepository))
161           config.as[DeploymentRepository](SnapshotRepository)
162         else null,
163         if (config.hasPath(SiteStr)) config.as[Site](SiteStr) else null,
164         if (config.hasPath(DownloadUrl)) config.getString(DownloadUrl)
165         else null,
166         if (config.hasPath(RelocationStr)) config.as[Relocation](RelocationStr)
167         else null,
168         if (config.hasPath(Status)) config.getString(Status)
169         else DistributionManagement.None
170       )
171     }
172 
173   /**
174     * Converts a Typesafe Config object to a Project case class which can
175     * produce Json or XML.
176     */
177   def readPOM(conf: Config): Project = conf.as[Project](ProjectStr)
178 
179   // allows reading of the Archive object from a Typesafe Config via Ficus
180   protected[unbound] def readArchiver(conf: Config): Archiver =
181     conf.as[Archiver](Archive)
182 }
183 
184 /** Static accessor to the Config -> Project case class conversion code */
185 object HoconReader extends HoconProjectReader
